r1520 | dahnke | 2019-11-19 22:52:09 +0100 (Di, 19 Nov 2019) | 49 lines

Changed paths:
M       CHANGES.txt
M       cat_conf_extopts.m
M       cat_conf_output.m
M       cat_defaults.m
M       cat_io_cmd.m
M       cat_main.m
M       cat_main_reportfig.m
M       cat_main_reportstr.m
M       cat_stat_marks.m
M       cat_surf_createCS.m
M       cat_surf_createCS2.m
M       cat_surf_display.m
M       cat_surf_fun.m
M       cat_surf_info.m
M       cat_surf_render2.m
M       cat_vol_pbt3.m
M       cat_vol_qa.m

(1) New:      Added two new runtime optimized collision corrections approaches in 
              cat_surf_fun that were called in cat_surf_createCS2. The first approach 
              (collcorr22) utilizes the CAT_selfintersect function that makes it  
              relativ slow (15 minutes), whereas the second approach (collcorr23) uses  
              the relative position map of PBT that makes it quite fast (2 minutes) but 
              less accurate. There is also an extended version (collcorr24) that
              optimize the surface based on the Ypp map and an even more accurate 
              version (collcorr25) that combines collcorr22 and collcorr24. 
(2) Changed:  Updated extended expert options for mesh resolution and collision 
              correction in cat_conf_extopts. 
(3) Changed:  Many corrections and updates in cat_surf_createCS2 and cat_surf_fun that 
              support the new self-intersection corrections and the evaluation of 
              surface reconstruction. Small adaptions of cat_surf_createCS to support
              the surface reconstruction measures but not for collision correction. 
(4) Changed:  Added output for surface measures in cat_main, cat_main_reportstr, 
              cat_main_reportfig, and cat_stat_marks.              
(5) Fixed:    Corrected atlas colormap naming bug, texture and surface handling in 
              cat_surf_render2. Little changes for PNG output. 
(6) New:      Added expert output options for the percentage position map and surface  
              measures in cat_conf_output, cat_defaults, and cat_surf_createCS2.
(7) Fixed:    Corrected setting in cerebellar surface reconstruction and added
              'cb' definition for reconstruction of both sides in cat_surf_info, 
              cat_main, cat_surf_display, and cat_main_createCS2. 
              Added standard resolution full cerebellar average surfaces 'cb.*'.
(8) Fixed:    Corrected output of surface defect maps in cat_surf_createCS2
              and added settings to cat_surf_info and cat_surf_render2.                
(9) New:      Added improved version of PBT (cat_surf_pbt2 and 3).

r1495 | gaser | 2019-08-14 18:18:11 +0200 (Mi, 14 Aug 2019) | 23 lines

Changed paths:
M       CHANGES.txt
M       Contents.m
M       cat_defaults.m
M       cat_surf_createCS.m
M       cat_surf_resamp.m
M       cat_surf_vol2surf.m
M       html/cat.html
 M      html/cat_statistics.html

(1) Changed: Implemented Freesurfer distance method Tfs, which is using the mean
    of the closest distances between surf1-surf2 and surf2-surf1. This reduces
    occurance of larger thickness values. For mapping the files ?h.pbt.* can be
    still used which are the old thickness metrics from PBT and are more
    appropriate for mapping 3D measures.
(2) Changed: cat_createCS is now using some experimental features that were 
    enabled before with the flag new_release. This includes check for self-
    intersection during surface refinement and mny smaller improvements during
    that step.
(3) Added: Added CAT binary CAT_SurfDistance which is estimating the new FS
    distance measure.

(1) Changed: Moved unused cat_vol_average.m to developer folder.
(2) Changed: Added option to reduce bounding box at final resolution level in 
    longitudinal registration.
(3) Added: Created new tool for calculating average of up to 5D data of same
    dimension and voxel size.
(4) Changed: Noise estimate in longitudinal tool is not used anymore because of
    instabilities for data from different scanners.
(5) Fixed: Use of Hessian matrix in longitudinal registration only if finite.
(6) Changed: Removed warp option for longitudinal pipeline because average
    deformation field will be now always written.
(7) Changed: Updated longitudinal pipeline w.r.t. to the actual changes. The 
    spatial registration is now estimated from the mean deformation field of
    all subjects instead of the deformation field of the mean image. This will 
    be more stable for larger changes between the time points.

                avoid deformation in these areas.

                Removed similar steps in cat_main and differentiate 
                between registration with(out) manual lesion data.
                Added handling for output of lesion maps.

                regions that sometimes strongly increased processing time
                (thanks to Gabriel Ziegler for pointing out that issue). 
5) Changed:     Updated automatic stroke lesion detection in 
                cat_vol_partvol by detecting large untypical CSF areas
                (and strongly (asymmetric) deformed regions), followed by
                a region-growing. The detection of asymmetric regions is 
                defined in cat_main but is inactive because it works only 
                in single cases yet.

r1325 | dahnke | 2018-06-20 19:57:53 +0200 (Mi, 20 Jun 2018) | 48 lines

Changed paths:
M       CHANGES.txt
M       cat_conf_extopts.m
M       cat_conf_tools.m
M       cat_defaults.m
M       cat_io_colormaps.m
M       cat_main.m
M       cat_main_registration.m
M       cat_run_job.m
M       cat_run_job1070.m
M       cat_surf_render2.m
M       cat_vol_partvol.m
M       ds.m
M       tbx_cfg_cat.m

PART A - WMHs: 
1) Changed:     Removed WMHCstr parameter from expert GUI to focus on the 
                standard case (changed to 0.5 in cat_defaults). 
2) Changed:     Moved WMHC correction after AMAP processing (cat_main). 
                WMH regions were now handled as GM in the initial AMAP 
                segmentation. After AMAP all GM voxels in WMH regions were
                set as GM (WMHC<2), WM (WMHC=2) or as extra class (WMHC=3).
                Added warnings in case of bad combinations of WMHC and
                WMHCstr that use no correction but output images.            
3) Changed:     The WMHs required an updated of the internal scaling of
                Yp0b in cat_main from 3 to 5 classes to have round uint8 
                values of a tissue class, ie. with a WM value of 255/5*3.                 

PART B - Lesion handling controlled by WMHC: 
1) New:         Added further cases to the WMHC parameter to handle the 
                lesion processing (WMHC=4). Added a simple detection of 
                very large lesion in cat_vol_partvol (WMHC=5).
2) New:         Added lesion handling by zero values in the original
                dataset that were now ignored in the Dartel/Shooting
                deformation process (cat_main_registration).               
3) New:         Because of the internal interpolation the detection of
                manual lesions (zero values in the brain) is located in 
                the cat_run_job(1070). 
4) New:         Added batch for lesion and brain masking (cat_conf_tools). 
                
PART C - Other changes: 
1) Changed:     Removed some gcutstr expert options because of to many 
                options and to unspecific/small/useless changes. 
2) Changed:     Small cleanup and modifications in cat_io_colormaps. 
3) Fixed:       Corrected small bug in cat_surf_render2.

r1248 | gaser | 2017-12-15 13:06:59 +0100 (Fr, 15 Dez 2017) | 27 lines

Changed paths:
M       CAT12-Manual.docx
M       CAT12-Manual.pdf
M       CHANGES.txt
M       Contents.m
M       cat_conf_stools.m
M       cat_surf_resamp.m
M       cat_surf_resamp_freesurfer.m
M       check_pipeline/batch_surface_pipeline.m
M       html/cat.html
M       html/cat_starting.html

(1) Fixed: Heat kernel smoothing was resolution dependent. Solved that issue
    and additionally replaced the weighting for filtering meshes with equal 
    weighting. Sigma is now the mean point distance. For cortical thickness 
    a good starting value is now 12-15mm, while other surface parameters 
    based on cortex folding (e.g. gyrification, cortical complexity) need a 
    larger filter size of about 20-25mm. Please update your scripts 
    and replace the old field "fwhm" by "fwhm_surf" and adapt the values.
(1) Changed: Again added option for 32k meshes because smoothing size
    is not correct for these meshes.
(2) Changed: Added warning if old scripts with "fwhm" filed are used in 
    cat_surf_resamp.m.
(3) Changed: The new name for resampled and smoothed surface data is not 
    containing "mm" anymore to indicate the filter size. This is also thought 
    to not mix data smoothed with the old and new smoothing method.

(1) Changed: Added remsampling to 32k mesh from Human Connectome Project
    (HCP). This allows faster and less memory demanding processing and 
    provides compatibility to the HCP. Another advantage is that left and 
    right hemispheres are aligned to optionally allow a direct comparison
    between hemispheres.
(2) Changed: Made all necessary functions compatible to 32k meshes.
(3) Added: New folders templates_surfaces_32k and atlases_surfaces_32k
(4) Fixed: Camlight and axes issue in cat_surf_results.m
(5) Changed: Renamed some files in templates_surfaces.

r1153 | dahnke | 2017-07-05 17:40:07 +0200 (Mi, 05 Jul 2017) | 23 lines

Changed paths:
M       CHANGES.txt
M       templates_1.50mm/Template_0_IXI555_MNI152_GS.nii
M       templates_1.50mm/Template_1_IXI555_MNI152_GS.nii
M       templates_1.50mm/Template_2_IXI555_MNI152_GS.nii
M       templates_1.50mm/Template_3_IXI555_MNI152_GS.nii
M       templates_1.50mm/Template_4_IXI555_MNI152_GS.nii

Changed:  Updated the Shooting template by a 1.5 mm version of the IXI template 
          processed with 1.0 mm and modified Shooting parameter with reduced 
          decay of coarse to fine schedule 
              lam = 1/3;  % default 0.5
          and adapted schedule parameter 
              d.sched = (d.sched - d.sched(end)) / diff([d.sched(end), ...
                         d.sched(1)])*(inter-1)+1;
          rather than
              d.sched = d.sched/d.sched(end);
          to a similar spectrum of values with smoother changes to increase the 
          amount of low frequency deformation and have smooth changes at all
          template stages. Keep in mind that even this template show much more
          anatomical details than the Dartel template, it requires less strong
          deformations to achieve this!

(1)  New:        Added detection of skull-stripped data to improve the affine
                 registration in cat_run_job. For initial affine registration a 
                 brain mask is applied to the template. Furthermore, the number 
                 of gaussian classes is corrected and checkt after the first 
                 SPM preprocessing. 
(2)  New:        If the initial affine registration failed and the AC is outside
                 of the image, than the COM is used to reinitialise the the
                 registration (cat_run_job). 
(3)  New:        Added biasfwhm modifier in case of strong inhomogeneities in 
                 cat_run_job.                
(4)  Changed:    Refined the fine affine registration in cat_run_job by further 
                 steps to reduce problems in R1 weighted scans and skull-striped
                 data. In case of skull-stripped data the brain mask is used. 
(4)  Changed:    Added cat_spm_affreg to avoid popup error message in case of 
                 initial affine registration errors that are maybe fixed by 
                 COM initialisation or spm_maff8. 
(5)  Changed:    Removed affreg case 'subj' regularisation because the results  
                 were equivalent with the case 'none' registration.  
                 Added comments for some parameter in cat_conf_opts. 
(6)  Fixed:      Corrected problems in cat_main_gintnorm and cat_main_LAS for  
                 inverse contrasts.
(7)  Fixed:      Corrected handling of template cases in cat_main_registration.
(8)  Fixed:      Replaced mean by cat_stat_nanmean in cat_tst_qa.
(9)  Changed:    Added grouping (gray background blocks) in cat_plot_boxplot.

A       html/images/neonates.png
M       html/style.css
M       internal/cat_vol_flipside.m

== New ==
(1) New*:      Added processing of images with BG<GM<WM<CSF contrast (neonates)
               as separate case that does not influence the default pipeline.
(2) New:       Added further preliminary validation results figures that are not
               linked in the help. 
   
== Parameterupdates ==              
(1) Changed:   opt.ngauss: 
               Updated SPM ngauss parameter in cat_defaults with only one      
               rather than three GM and WM classes because it was more stable   
               onthe BWP and real Datasets.  More than one GM and WM gaussian   
               peaks seams to bet better in case of inverse data (T2/PD). 
               Hence, an automatically switch to more than three GM and WM 
               peaks is added in the cat_run_job. 
(2) Changed:   extopts.resval & extopts.restype: 
               Increased the upper limit of the internal interpolation to 0.5 mm  
               rather than 1.0 mm (resval = [0.5 0.3]) and add 1.0 mm as minimum
               resolution to improve the results in case of anisotropic high- 
               resolution data (e.g., 0.5x0.5x1.5 mm) but also of low resolution
               data of the default interpolation option (restype = 'best'). 
(3) Changed:   opt.biasreg, opt.biasfwhm & opt.biasstr:
               Added opts.biasstr parameter to the cat_default-file and to  
               the GUI to have a simple control parameter for inhomogeneity 
               correction that controls the SPM preprocessing parameter 
               opts.biasreg and opts.biasfwhm that were removed at once 
               from the expert GUI. 
(4) Changed:   Corrected LASstr parameter to give optimal results for 0.5.               
(5) Changed:   opts.warpreg:
               Removed opts.warpreg parameter from expert GUI because our test
               indicated no useful changes with no general effects and only
               worse results in single cases.
(6) Changed:   Added additional sub parameter for lab operation in cat_vol_morph
               to allow more than one large cluster.
       
               
== Other Updates ==              
(1) Changed:   Replace old SPM tissue threshold estimation by the @-function 
               "clsint" in cat_main, cat_main_gintnorm.  
(2) Changed:   Added transparency and saturation parameter to cat_plot_boxplot. 
(3) Changed:   Forced low change rate for first Shooting template to improve 
               Shooting quality of lower regstr values.
(4) Changed:   Added resolution dependency for cleanup of the initial SPM 
               segmentation to avoid problems in case of low resolution.
              
(5) Changed:   Use realignment in "cat_tst_calc_kappa" in case of different 
               resolution only if realign parameter is true. Otherwise, imcalc
               is used directly.
(6) Changed:   Updated help texts in cat_conf_opts and reduce the amount of 
               control parameters. 
(7) Changed:   Added resolution dependency in cat_vol_sanlm to reduce the amout
               of filtering in low resolution data. 


== Bug fixes ==
(1) Fixed:     Corrected bugs in cat_run_APP_init.
(2) Fixed:     Corrected Ym intensity scaling problem in cat_main_LAS.
(3) Fixed:     Corrected index error in cat_surf_smooth.
               Thanks to Björn Horing for pointing out this bug.
(4) Fixed:     Corrected WMH volume output in CAT report and XML file.
               Thanks to M.H.T. Zwartbol for pointing out this bug.
(5) Fixed:     Corrected simultan output of modulated data in expert mode in 
               cat_io_writenii and cat_main.
               Thanks to Felix Hoffstaedter for pointing out this limitation.
(6) Fixed:     Corrected typo in SPM PBT figure.
(7) Fixed:     Special case in PBT data processing of binary data.

(2) Changed:  Refined smoothing in "cat_surf_createCS" to reduce artifacts 
              in noise data or by meninges.
(3) Changed:  Refined greater apes CAT atlas.

(1) Changed:    Separate the bias, noise and intensity corrected image (Ym)  
                into two subversion with global (Ym) and local (Ymi) intensity 
                normalization. The Ym is more reasonable for myelination 
                analysis, whereas the Ymi more sensible for the tissue classes.
                Also for Ym LAS is used to correct reminding WM inhomogeneities.
                The output of the local normalized image is only assessable via
                cat_defaults (cat.output.las) and expert GUI.
                The CAT ROIs will extract the intensities of the Ym rather of 
                the Ymi. The CAT report now shows the Ym rather than the Ymi.
(2) Changed:    Added ROI menu to expert GUI.
(3) Fixed:      Volume creation error in TCA part of cat_surf_createCS.
(4) Fixed:      Update version of cat_surf_render.
(5) Changed:    Added surface type check in cat_surf_resamp to ignore
                '.central.' and '.sphere.'.                
(6) Fixed:      Fast correction of side flip in animal atlas maps.

          area estimation, hull creation for surfaces, and volume rendering.

          cat_surf_epivolsurf.

          datatypes, e.g. to save disk memory.

          Windows and Linux.
Changed*: Set cat.extopts.resval parameter to avoid interpolation. 
Added*:   Intensity scaling functions for cat_surf_display (cat_surf_render).
Added*:   Material and lighting options for cat_surf_display (cat_surf_render).
Added:    Added lazy processing for EXPERTs for CAT segmentation. 
          This allows to avoid the preprocessing, if the same parameter are used
          and the expected results exist.  
          This function is useful for problems in large datasets, if the 
          preprocessing of some subjects or complete jobs failed by internal 
          (small cat errors) or external (matlab or systems error, server errors). 
Added:    EXPERT function and files to flip the side of the surface.
Fixed:    Some HTML help layout problems.
Fixed:    Small changes for CSF thresholds in cat_main_gintnorm and cat_main_LAS.

              the standard CAT pipeline.

              on a basic level.

              default registration to correct problems especially in skull-
              stripped images.

              blood vessels. Corrected initial Ym background value estimation.

              SPM peaks of Ym differ to much.

New:      Added Non-local-means upsampling (NLMUS) function cat_vol_nlmus.
          NLMUS is relatively slow (~10 minutes for 1x1x3 NIH image, ~40 minutes
          for 0.6x0.6x1.8 reduced Winterburn image), but I think it do a great
          job especially for anisotropic data. It does not work in label images
          such as the p0*.nii or atlas maps.
New:      Added internal c-function for NLMUS for mac/linux (working) and 
          windows (not yet tested). Added code in compile function.
New:      Added internal function to reduce template surfaces for faster tests. 
          Although the reduction works correct, moste surface processing
          functions were not faster.

r808 | dahnke | 2015-12-03 10:19:36 +0100 (Do, 03 Dez 2015) | 31 lines

Changed paths:
M       CHANGES.txt
M       cat_main.m
M       cat_run.m
M       cat_surf_createCS.m
M       cat_surf_display.m
M       cat_surf_vol2surf.m
A       internal/cat_vol_atlas.m
 M      templates_1.50mm

New:     Added internal cat_vol_atlas function to normalize, optimize and merge
         common atlas datasets such as AAL, IBSR, HAMMERS, ANATOMY, MORI, LPBA40,
         Neuromorphometrics,  ... 
         The function optimize, normalize and merge the atlas ROIs of one or 
         multiple subjects as 4D probability map to create a single 3D atlas map. 
         It use CAT preprocessing and median filtering to optimize and normalize
         the individual atlas ROIs and try to rename the ROI names given by the 
         CSV Files by a dictionary. 
         The function is still in development, the principle idea works, but 
         the naming is not correct for all regions. 
Changed: Replace SPM PS by MATLAB print function to write CAT report as PDF, 
         because the PS is outdated and does not work with surfaces.  
Changed: Common print structure in cat_surf_display and cat_main.
Changed: Added SPM command line link for cat_surf_vol2surf output, if job.verb 
         is >0.  
Fixed:   Corrected surface colormap and scaling after changing to SPM gray.
Fixed:   Double surface output in CAT report.
Fixed:   Changed thickness field estimation and fixed writing in XML file. 
Comment: Added ;; in MATLAB code to mark special lines to jump in the editor.

r759 | dahnke | 2015-11-09 10:38:54 +0100 (Mo, 09 Nov 2015) | 28 lines

(1)  Dartel resolution limit as minimum voxel size only in best resolution case.
(2)  Set millimeter-based boxing rather in voxel-based for brain boundary box. 
(3)  Changes in the cg_vbm_defaults output definition. Replaced affine entry by
     dartel entry. 
(4)  Added ISARNLM (Iterative Spatial Adaptive multi-Resolution Non Local Means)
     filter for high resolution data (<0.7 mm) to deal better with noise in 
     interpolation, parallel-imaging and band-width artifacts.
(5)  Updated APP processing and options. Corrected problems of data with strong 
     bias (7T) or/and large ventricle (IXI175).  
(6)  Added cls 4-6 output for template generation. 
(7)  Corrected using of SPM class values (minimum fraction has to be 10%).
(8)  Corrected command line output.
(9)  Unready optimizations of the WMH correction.

r756 | dahnke | 2015-10-20 18:30:50 +0200 (Di, 20 Okt 2015) | 25 lines

Changed paths:
M       CHANGES.txt
M       cg_vbm_batch.m
M       cg_vbm_defaults.m
M       cg_vbm_extopts.m

M       cg_vbm_write.m
M       ds.m
M       vbm_surf_display.m
M       vbm_surf_resamp.m
M       vbm_vol_partvol.m

(1)  Added affine preprocessing (APP=Affine PreProcessing) in cg_vbm_run_job 
     with APP parameter in cg_vbm_defaults and experimental expert GUI option. 
     APP include a bias rough bias correction and brain extraction to support 
     untypical cases (non-human/neonates) with registration problems. 
     This also include changes in preprocessing 1 part in the cg_vbm_write.
(2)  Removed high resolution voxel size limit.
(3)  Corrected tiny error that ignored rigid data output parameter.
(4)  Deactivate divergence variable in LAS and set lower upper threshold for GM
     because of problems in high contrast data with strong GM variation where
     low GM intensities were not corrected and therefore misclassified as CSF.
     Further tiny changes to stabilize the CSF/background field. 
(5)  Improved segmentation of subcortical regions in vbm_vol_partvol.

r707 | dahnke | 2015-08-17 14:22:10 +0200 (Mo, 17 Aug 2015) | 22 lines

Changed paths:
M       ds.m
M       vbm_stat_marks.m
M       vbm_tst_calc_kappa.m
M       vbm_tst_qa.m

(1)  Added realignment function in "vbm_tst_calc_kappa".
(2)  Major update of the QA estimation "vbm_tst_qa" and "vbm_stat_marks":
     - The last changes (R686-R690) did not show improvements in all test areas. 
       There were strong age effects, and only partial improvements that did not 
       fit to the increased complexity and run time of the code.
       Therefore, the function was rebuild based on R650 and optimized by the 
       best ideas of versions R665-R682 to reduce variation between different 
       preprocessing methods (SPM8/12,FSL,VBM8/12) that were a strong problem in
       version R650. 
     - Most mentionable is that the focus of noise estimation moved from WM to
       CSF (if possible) to avoid aging effects, where the age depended changes
       of the WM structure can be misinterpreted as noise. Although, the methods
       to avoid these regions work in most cases, some kind of noise/movement
       artifacts showed a similar pattern that lead to an underestimation of 
       noise in these cases.

r698 | dahnke | 2015-06-02 10:40:10 +0200 (Di, 02 Jun 2015) | 41 lines

Changed paths:
M       cg_vbm_stools.m
M       cg_vbm_write.m
A       templates_surfaces/lh.central.freesurfer.gii
A       templates_surfaces/rh.central.freesurfer.gii

M       vbm_surf_rename.m
M       vbm_surf_render.m
M       vbm_surf_resample.m
M       vbm_surf_smooth.m

(1)  Changes for MT-image processing in "cg_vbm_write":
     - Deactivate SPM MRF filter to 0, because it removed to much informations. 
     - Corrected global intensity scaling errors for negative values in MT 
       contrast images ("vbm_pre_gintnorm" in "cg_vbm_write").
(2)  LAS updates in "cg_vbm_write":
     - Added estimation for the difference between cortical and subcortical GM 
       for further automatic control of the LAS filter strength. 
       MT data with lesser variation of GM tissue intensities will have a lower
       CV value and require less adaption.
     - Replaced TPM by Dartel template map.  
     - Added divergence skeleton for more better distance based cortical GM 
       detection and correction.
(3)  Added a try-catch block for surface creation in "cg_vbm_write".
(4)  Updates for surface rendering:
     - Renamed gyrus and sulcus width surface textures filenames according to 
       "thickness" texture filename in "gyruswidth", "gyruswidthWM", and
       "sulcuswidth".
     - Corrected print problems in "vbm_surf_display" (lighting does not work 
       with phong) and prepare print function. 
     - Set finer colormaps (256 values rather than 32).
     - Added multi-surface display in "vbm_surf_render" and "vbm_surf_display".
(5)  Corrected output directory and progress bar errors in "vbm_surf_calc".
(6)  Added FreeSurfer average surfaces "[lr]h.central.freesurfer.gii".
(7)  Added lazy processing in "vbm_surf_resample" and "vbm_surf_smooth" 
     (estimation only if files does not exist).

r674 | dahnke | 2015-02-24 15:59:47 +0100 (Di, 24 Feb 2015) | 51 lines

Changed paths:
 M      .
M       cg_vbm_defaults.m
A       cg_vbm_defaults_template_humanIXI555.m
M       cg_vbm_run_job.m
M       cg_vbm_write.m
A  +    html/vbm12_instruction_templates.html
 M      templates_animals
A       templates_animals/cg_vbm_defaults_template_primate130.m
A       templates_animals/cg_vbm_defaults_template_primate15.m
A       templates_animals/cg_vbm_defaults_template_primate400.m
A       templates_animals/cg_vbm_defaults_template_primate45.m
M       vbm_io_cgw2seg.m
M       vbm_io_img2nii.m
M       vbm_io_remat.m
M       vbm_set_cg_vbm_defaults.m
M       vbm_stat_marks.m
M       vbm_tst_CJV.m
M       vbm_tst_qa.m
M       vbm_vol_approx.m
M       vbm_vol_correct_slice_scaling.m

Major changes:
(1)  Corrected "median"-problem in "vbm_pre_gintnorm" in "cg_vbm_write". 
     The median was used to estimate tissue peaks, but lightly different mask 
     in different OS leaded to different tissue peaks that lead to stronger 
     differences between Linux and Windows/Mac. Used rounding operations (10^-5)
     to guaranty similar values.  
(2)  Corrected error in CSF/BG estimation in "vbm_pre_LAS2" in "cg_vbm_write"
     that emphasize background noise.
     Added code to improve the cortical GM segmentation, especially after the 
     bias correction (LAS-WM threshold).
(3)  Changed handling of the MRF filter after spm-preprocessing2 in 
     "cg_vbm_write". 
(4)  Large update for "vbm_vol_correct_slice_scaling". 
     Added automatic detection of slice and iteration criteria and validate the 
     function for simulated artifacts in the brain web phantom. Added the private 
     script "vbm_tst_BWPsliceartifact" that modifies and test images.
     
     
Minor changes:
(1)  Added help and small corrections in "cg_io_cgw2seg" and "vbm_io_img2nii.
(2)  Updated "vbm_io_remat" and added help.
(3)  Updated species specific processing in "vbm_tst_qa".
(4)  Added new "cg_vbm_defaults" for primates brain volume based primate 
     templates and html-help file.
(5)  Added code to compare the preprocessing steps on different operating 
     systems in "cg_vbm_run_job" and "cg_vbm_run_job".  
(*)  Further small corrections.

M       vbm_vol_pbt.m
M       vbm_vol_pbtp.mexmaci64
M       vbm_vol_resize.m
M       vbm_vol_simgrow.mexmaci64

This update contain a lot of changes, corrections and updates for large parts of
the segmentation pipeline.
(1)  Added symbolic link support for "distribute_to_server.sh".
(2)  Optimized skull-stripping and removed "gcutcsf" parameter.
     Verified behavior of 'gcutstr' in range between 0 and 1.   
(3)  Merged B3C inhomogeneity correction and the Local Adaptive Segmentation 
     (LAS) with direct access to atlas data. 
     Removed 'Final LAS corrections' and 'Final Masking' function and options.
     Verified behavior of 'LASstr' in range between 0 and 1.   
(4)  Extended "BVC" to "BVCstr" parameter for further control of the blood 
     vessel correction, with 0 for no correction.
     Verified behavior of 'BVCstr' in range between 0 and 1.   
(5)  Updated and tested inverse pipeline 'extopts.INV' that is now part of the 
     global intensity normalization function, including a small bias WM based 
     inhomogeneity correction to avoid inversion problems.   
     Verified behavior for T2 and PD datasets, with good results for good data. 
(6)  Added new improved cleanup routine ('extopts.cleanup==3'). 
(7)  Added VBM warnings to 'vbm12*.mat' (QA.SW.vbm_warnings) and display them 
     in the final report (not tested yet).  
(8)  Added old ORNLM filter for noise removal after intensity scaling. The 
     strength of the filter is controlled by a CJV like measure to assure 
     smooth tissues. Using the NLM filter should work better than only a 
     stronger MRF filter! Filter strength is limited by a sixth of tissue 
     contrast. 
     
Unsolved problems, warnings, and errors:
(1)  Unsolved errors for "extopts.kmeans=1" with AMAP segmentation errors.
(2)  Unsolved errors for surface generation "Cat_SeparatePolygon" or "reducepatch" under Windows with incorrect  
     values of the vertices of the the surface faces.
(3)  Images with low NCR/high CNR trend to have local WM overestimation. 
     The brainstem is a little bit to white and lead to WM overestimations in 
     the cerebellum (see also BWP_MS2_Collins_t1_pn9_rf100pA.nii).
     > Check LAS bias correction. 
(4)  To strong noise correction in high resolution images (ORNLM strength). 
(5)  PD/T2 pipeline:
     > The GM/CSF boundary/peak estimation in low contrast images (CSF~GM) 
       requires stronger connection of SPM-segmentation and intensity information 
       (see XNAT-flash3 subjects / BWP_HC_Collins_pd_pn[3|9]_rf[040|100]pA ).
     > Some images show background inversion problems and requires blood vessel 
       correction (NIH-T2 subjects).
     > Evaluation for IXI and NIH data in relation to T1 segmentation required

r535 | dahnke | 2013-12-04 18:51:36 +0100 (Mi, 04 Dez 2013) | 55 lines

Changed paths:
M       AmapMex.c
M       AmapMex.mexmaci64
M       CAT.maci64/CAT_FixTopology
M       cg_vbm_batch.m
M       cg_vbm_defaults.m

M       tbx_cfg_vbm.m

A       vbm_stat_nanmean.m
A       vbm_stat_nanmedian.m
A       vbm_stat_nanstd.m
M       vbm_surf_createCS.m
M       vbm_tst_SRS.m
M       vbm_tst_calc_bias.m
M       vbm_tst_calc_kappa.m
M       vbm_tst_pre.m
M       vbm_tst_qa_groups.m
M       vbm_tst_staple_multilabels.m
M       vbm_tst_t1qa.m
M       vbm_vol_atlas.m
M       vbm_vol_average.m
M       vbm_vol_iscale.m
M       vbm_vol_nanmean3.m
M       vbm_vol_partvol.m
M       vbm_vol_resize.m
M       vbm_vol_smooth3X.m
M       vbm_vol_t1qacalc.m

(1)  Renamed 'vbm_*.ps' to 'vbmreport_*' for correct spm-sorting of filetypes.
(2)  Added experimental WM hyperintensity (WMH) correction (extopts.WMHC), WMH 
     detection (vbm_vol_partioning) and WMH correction (in cg_write_vol).
     WARNING: This code is in a very early development step and do not work yet
              and default extopts.WMHC=0!
(3)  Added variable (extopts.gcutCSF) to modify the gcut+ skull-stripping to 
     obtain more surrounding CSF.  
     WARNING: CSF contrast depend strongly on the MR-protocol, and high contrast 
              images may have a similar intensity of CSF, background and bone!
              Therefore CSF segment quality can vary strongly for multi-protocol
              VBM, and extopts.gcutCSF may be turned off!
              Added a warning for this case.
(4)  Updated mean tissue intensity estimation for global intensity correction.
(5)  Replaced MATLAB toolbox nan-functions and calls by own methods:
     vbm_stat_nanmean,vbm_stat_nanstd,vbm_stat_nanmedian
(6)  Created subfunctions for longer parts in cg_vbm_write to increase readability
     may with some cost of memory (but this should be no critical part):
      (a) the global intensity normalization (vbm_pre_gintnorm)
      (b) fast partitioning for major brain structures (vbm_pre_fastpart)
      (c) brain and maximum-based bias correction B3C (vbm_pre_B3C)
      (d) calc preprocessing expectation map (vbm_qa_calcTE)
(7)  Created subfunctions for often used parts in cg_vbm_write:
      (a) egde image Yg (vbm_vol_grad)
      (b) fast divergence image Ydiv (vbm_vol_div)     
(8)  Corrected output for atlas, te, pc images in tbx_cfg_vbm and cg_vbm_batch.

r490 | dahnke | 2013-05-24 10:02:52 +0200 (Fr, 24 Mai 2013) | 20 lines

Changed paths:
M       cg_vbm_defaults.m
M       cg_vbm_run.m
M       cg_vbm_write.m
M       vbm_vol_partvol.m

This is just a sub-step with experimental elements that I want to save before
I change the next things...
(1) To obtain a better inhomogeneity correction SPM-default Parameter were 
    changed (biasfwhm=30, samp=2), with better results but higher calculation
    time. Strong improvements for highres (Magdeburg7T and HR075) and lowres
    images (NIH1394). This works better than the additional maximum based
    correction and I will remove/uncomment the maximum correction. :/
(2) The Partition work not bad, but it is now very slow (>1 minute) and I have
    optimize many substeps (mostly by resizing to lower resolutions).
(3) Correction of the tissue peak estimation for the global intensity 
    normalization for images with WM lessions (OASIS0031) that lead to error in 
    the skull-stripping.
(4) Skull-Stripping of this version is still to aggressive.

r487 | dahnke | 2013-05-15 11:20:44 +0200 (Mi, 15 Mai 2013) | 35 lines

Changed paths:
M       cg_vbm_run.m
M       cg_vbm_write.m
M       vbm_stat_marks.m
M       vbm_vol_partvol.m

(1) Moving of the partitioning routines before the skull-stripping, to use the 
    atlas map for skull-stripping to allow regional different growing rates.
    Although, now only SPM standard normalization is used, I expect a similar 
    accuracy, because the partitioning use the atlas mostly for initialization  
    followed by a region growing. The partitioning still requires more work to 
    get smoother segments without removing anatomical details. 
(2) Maximum-based bias correction and intensity scaling for global and local
    segmentation.
(3) Less aggressive local adaption with a stronger relation to SPM classes.
(4) Correct an SPM label error, where intracranial BG was labeled as CSF that
    produce CSF mean intensities that were to close to the BG intensity and
    CSF was detected as low GM. Correct also the other "direction" where CGM
(5) The partitioning routine allows now a direct mapping of the basal ganglia
    for maximum-based bias correction and local adaptive segmentation.   
(6) New skull-stripping routine in the LAS pipeline (alpha status) with a harder
    brain extraction to reduce meninges and blood vessels that needs to be a 
    little bit smoother:
    
               DICE     FP    FN
      VBM12i:  0.9632   4437  83478
      VBM12:   0.9720  21337  46823
      
(7) Deactivated BVC for inverse contrast.
(8) Command window output updates:
    - Added colored output for the filename output.
    - Added computation times for preprocessing steps.
    - Added final output with total computation time and with short QA results.
    - Final reduction of Dartel command window output.

This update include a lot of new methods and function mostly with alpa-status.
(1) Added a global intensity normalisation (mg*.nii) with WM=1, GM=2/3, CSF=1/3.
(2) Added a new local adaptive segmentation (LAD) pipeline with local corrected, 
    brain masked version (ml*.nii) of the T1 input with WM=1, GM=2/3, CSF=1/3.
    The new pipeline include:
    - local adaptive tissue peak estimation for lower area PVE especially in
      deep GM structures
    - local sharpening for thin gyral WM structures
    - new final skull-stripping
    - (blood vessel correction)
(3) Added GM thickness estimation (th1*.nii) for RAW-resolution that still 
    requires the interpolation for full quality.
(4) Prepare segmentation for major brain regions and sides (l1*.nii).
(5) Added a preprocessing change map to map changes in the preprocessing to 
    identify problematic data and processing. 
(6) Added XML import/export/update function for MATLAB structures. Replace text
    by XML export (*_seg8.txt > vbm_*.xml). 
(7) Added the "vbm_*_" prefix for some function.
(8) Starts replacement of cg_morph_vol by vbm_vol_morph.
(9) Preparing a write function to write a image in different spaces.
(10) Update of the GUI and variables for the additional functions.
